    432: Champions League Betting
    434: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

Cristiano Ronaldo is the competition's all-time top-scorer with 140 goals in 183 appearances for Manchester United, Real Madrid and Juventus.

    450: FA Cup Final
    452: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.
    454: The FA Cup is the only competition in the country where non-league minnows can end up going against some of the biggest and best clubs in the world. We offer a huge range of FA Cup betting markets from the first round right through to the semi-finals and final at Wembley Stadium.

452: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.
    454: The FA Cup is the only competition in the country where non-league minnows can end up going against some of the biggest and best clubs in the world. We offer a huge range of FA Cup betting markets from the first round right through to the semi-finals and final at Wembley Stadium.
    456: Qualification for the FA Cup begins as early as August with the extra preliminary round. The first round proper takes place in November, with Premier League and Championship teams entering the competition at the third-round stage in January. The final is slated for May.

    1016: Champions League Betting
    1018: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    1036: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.

    1342: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    1360: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. 1360: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.
    1362: The FA Cup is the only competition in the country where non-league minnows can end up going against some of the biggest and best clubs in the world. We offer a huge range of FA Cup betting markets from the first round right through to the semi-finals and final at Wembley Stadium.
    1364: Qualification for the FA Cup begins as early as August with the extra preliminary round. The first round proper takes place in November, with Premier League and Championship teams entering the competition at the third-round stage in January. The final is slated for May.

    1672: Champions League Betting
    1674: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    1692: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet.     1996: Champions League Betting
    1998: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    2562: Champions League Betting
    2564: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    3144: Champions League Betting
    3146: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    3164: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet.     3710: Champions League Betting
    3712: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    3728: FA Cup Final
    3730: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet.     4278: Champions League Betting
    4280: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    4848: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    5424: Champions League Betting
    5426: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    6002: Champions League Betting
    6004: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.
    6006: At William Hill, we have pre-tournament odds under the Champions League betting, plus a host of other odds throughout the tournament, from group winners to top goalscorers.
    6008: Our traders also have options for the Europa League, Europa Conference League, European Super Cup and the FIFA Club World Cup: whatever cup competition you're looking for, William Hill have a market for it.
    6010: Real Madrid are the most successful team in the history of the Champions League,The most successful English team is Liverpool, who have won it six times, most recently in 2019. Cristiano Ronaldo is the competition's all-time top-scorer with 140 goals in 183 appearances for Manchester United, Real Madrid and Juventus.

    6020: FA Cup Final
    6022: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.
    6024: The FA Cup is the only competition in the country where non-league minnows can end up going against some of the biggest and best clubs in the world. We offer a huge range of FA Cup betting markets from the first round right through to the semi-finals and final at Wembley Stadium.

6022: The showpiece event of the English football season, the FA Cup final is one of the oldest and most-watched cup competitions on the planet. The FA Cup started in 1871 and features over 600 teams trying to make it down to the final 124 at the first-round stage, on the road to a Wembley final.
    6024: The FA Cup is the only competition in the country where non-league minnows can end up going against some of the biggest and best clubs in the world. We offer a huge range of FA Cup betting markets from the first round right through to the semi-finals and final at Wembley Stadium.
    6026: Qualification for the FA Cup begins as early as August with the extra preliminary round. The first round proper takes place in November, with Premier League and Championship teams entering the competition at the third-round stage in January. The final is slated for May.

    6051: Accumulators
    6053: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    6059: As well as a huge range of pre-match markets, you can also bet in-play on matches that have already started. Just watched a team go 1-0 down and fancy them to pull off a comeback? You can place a bet as the action unfolds with our massive selection of live betting markets.

6045: Total number of goals - will there be over or under a set line?
    6046: Football accumulators, doubles and trebles
    6047: Doubles & Trebles
    6049: Fancy two or three teams to win? You can bet on both or all three happening for the chance to get even bigger odds by creating a double or treble.
    6051: Accumulators
    6053: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.
